<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предзнаменование.html>предзнаменова́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predznamenovánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предзнаменование.html>предзнаменова́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предзнаменование.html>предзнаменова́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предзнаменование.html>предзнаменова́ний</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предложение.html>предложе́ние</a> (1349)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предложить.html>предложи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предложение.html>предложе́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predložénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предложение.html>предложе́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предложение.html>предложе́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предложение.html>предложе́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>offer</li>
<li>suggestion, proposal (<i>also: marriage proposal</i>), proposition</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">commerce</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> supply</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">parliamentary action</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> motion</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sentence, clause</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предложить.html>предложи́ть</a> (633)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пред-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pred-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ложи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предложить.html>предложи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predložítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предлагать.html>предлага́ть</a></b>)

<li>to propose, to suggest, to proposition</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предместье.html>предме́стье</a> (18650)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">przedmieście</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предместье.html>предме́стье</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predméstʹje</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предместье.html>предме́стья</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предместье.html>предме́стья</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предместье.html>предме́стий</a></b>)

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">przedmiot</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">subject; object</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself a calque of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">objectum</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предметный.html>предме́тный</a> (25527)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предмет.html>предме́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predmét</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">object, subject</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предметный.html>предме́тный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predmétnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> subject
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предметный.html>предме́тный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:каталог.html>катало́г</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predmétnyj</b> katalóg</i> ― <span class="e-translation">subject catalog</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> object
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предметный.html>предме́тный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:урок.html>уро́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predmétnyj</b> urók</i> ― <span class="e-translation">object lesson</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предметный.html>предме́тное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стекло.html>стекло́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predmétnoje</b> stekló</i> ― <span class="e-translation">microscope slide</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>material, physical</li></ol>

***предназначить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предназначить.html>предназна́чить</a> (4190)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пред-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pred-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назначить.html>назна́чить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naznáčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предназначить.html>предназна́чить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prednaznáčitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">предназнача́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to appropriate</li>
<li>to assign</li>
<li>to design (for a specific purpose)</li>
<li>to intend (for), to destine (for / to); to mean (for); to set aside (for), to earmark (for)</li>
<li>to consign; to reserve</li></ol>

***предопределённый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предопределить.html>предопределённый</a> (14290)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предопределить.html>предопредели́ть</a> (14290)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пред-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pred-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:определить.html>определи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">opredelítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предопределить.html>предопредели́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predopredelítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предопределять.html>предопределя́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to predetermine, to predestine, to foreordain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предопределить.html>предопредели́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:исход.html>исхо́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predopredelítʹ</b> isxód</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to predetermine the outcome</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***предопределять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предопределять.html>предопределя́ть</a> (29276)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предопределить.html>предопредели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predopredelítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предопределять.html>предопределя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predopredeljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предопределить.html>предопредели́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to predetermine, to predestine, to foreordain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предопределять.html>предопределя́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:исход.html>исхо́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predopredeljátʹ</b> isxód</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to predetermine the outcome</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***предоставить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предоставить.html>предоста́вить</a> (3491)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">прѣдъставити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prědŭstaviti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">прѣдъ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prědŭ-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">ставити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">staviti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставить.html>предоста́вить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predostávitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставлять.html>предоставля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to let have <i>(to)</i>, to leave <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставить.html>предоста́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predostávitʹ</b> slóvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to let have the floor</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to give <i>(to)</i>, to render <i>(to)</i>, to grant <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставить.html>предоста́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:распоряжение.html>распоряже́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predostávitʹ</b> v rasporjažénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put at smb.'s disposal</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставить.html>предоста́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свобода.html>свобо́ду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:действие.html>де́йствий</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predostávitʹ</b> svobódu déjstvij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give free hand</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставить.html>предоста́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:полный.html>по́лную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свобода.html>свобо́ду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predostávitʹ</b> pólnuju svobódu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give free rein</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставить.html>предоста́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:чрезвычайный.html>чрезвыча́йные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полномочие.html>полномо́чия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predostávitʹ</b> črezvyčájnyje polnomóčija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to confer emergency powers</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставить.html>предоста́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:избирательный.html>избира́тельные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>права</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predostávitʹ</b> izbirátelʹnyje prava</i> ― <span class="e-translation">enfranchise</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставить.html>предоста́вить</a></b> заём</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predostávitʹ</b> zajóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to grant a loan</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставить.html>предоста́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кредит.html>креди́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predostávitʹ</b> kredít</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give credit</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставить.html>предоста́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:возможность.html>возмо́жность</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predostávitʹ</b> vozmóžnostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give an opportunity, to give a chance</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставить.html>предоста́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:убежище.html>убе́жище</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predostávitʹ</b> ubéžišče</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to grant asylum</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставить.html>предоста́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>самому</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predostávitʹ</b> samomu sebé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to leave on his own, to leave to his own resources</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***предоставлять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предоставлять.html>предоставля́ть</a> (7474)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставить.html>предоста́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predostávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставлять.html>предоставля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predostavljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставить.html>предоста́вить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to let have <i>(to)</i>, to leave <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставлять.html>предоставля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predostavljátʹ</b> slóvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to let have the floor</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to give <i>(to)</i>, to render <i>(to)</i>, to grant <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставлять.html>предоставля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:распоряжение.html>распоряже́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predostavljátʹ</b> v rasporjažénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put at smb.'s disposal</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставлять.html>предоставля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свобода.html>свобо́ду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:действие.html>де́йствий</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predostavljátʹ</b> svobódu déjstvij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give free hand</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставлять.html>предоставля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:полный.html>по́лную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свобода.html>свобо́ду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predostavljátʹ</b> pólnuju svobódu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give free rein</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставлять.html>предоставля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:чрезвычайный.html>чрезвыча́йные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полномочие.html>полномо́чия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predostavljátʹ</b> črezvyčájnyje polnomóčija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to confer emergency powers</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставлять.html>предоставля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:избирательный.html>избира́тельные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>права</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predostavljátʹ</b> izbirátelʹnyje prava</i> ― <span class="e-translation">enfranchise</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставлять.html>предоставля́ть</a></b> заём</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predostavljátʹ</b> zajóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to grant a loan</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставлять.html>предоставля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кредит.html>креди́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predostavljátʹ</b> kredít</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give credit</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставлять.html>предоставля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:возможность.html>возмо́жность</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predostavljátʹ</b> vozmóžnostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give an opportunity, to give a chance</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставлять.html>предоставля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:убежище.html>убе́жище</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predostavljátʹ</b> ubéžišče</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to grant asylum</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предоставлять.html>предоставля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>самому</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predostavljátʹ</b> samomu sebé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to leave on his own, to leave to his own resources</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
